Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	*******************************************************************************
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	UseCase for MSP430.dll                                                         
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	Demo application for identifying an MSP430 device and compare the read         
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	parameters of the device properties structure against the parameters given by  
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	the DeviceID number through MSP430_Device().                                   
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	Usage: MSP430Flasher.exe [OPTIONS]                                             
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -n DEVICE NAME              specifies the name of the targeted device.        
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (required)                                        
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -o L | C                    specifies the desired mode (only for L092 device).
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (use L for L092 and C for C092-emulator mode)     
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -l PASSWORD LENGTH          specifies the length of the JTAG password.        
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (in words, if any, default: 0)                    
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -p JTAG PASSWORD            specifies the JTAG password (form: 0x...).        
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (if any, default: no password)                    
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -i (TI)USB | LPTn | COMn    specifies the connection interface.               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (default: TIUSB (=USB))                           
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -m JTAG | SBW2 | SBW4 |     specifies the communication mode                  
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	    AUTO                     (JTAG or Spy-Bi-Wire. default: AUTO)              
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -r [filenname,mem_sect]     specifies a memory section to read from and a file
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (txt/hex) to write to. mem_sect: RAM, INFO, MAIN, 
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             BSL                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -w filenname                specifies a file (txt/hex) for device programming.
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -b                          unlocks BSL memory for writing                    
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (use only with -w switch)                         
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -u                          unlocks InfoA memory for writing                  
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (use only with -w switch)                         
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -e ERASE_ALL | ERASE_MAIN | specifies erase mode before programming.          
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	    ERASE_SEGMENT            (use only with -w switch, default: ERASE_ALL but  
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             ERASE_MAIN for the L092 devices)                  
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -v                          triggers verification after programming           
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (use only with -w switch)                         
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -z [exit_spec,...]          specifies state of device on exit                 
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             (view available 'exit_spec's using -x switch)     
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -g                          switches log OFF (default: ON)                    
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -q                          triggers QUIET MODE (no system messages displayed)
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -d [breakpoint addresses]   specifies addresses for hardware breakpoints and  
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                             triggers RUN_TO_BREAKPOINT mode after initialization
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -t timeout_in_ms            specifies the breakpoint timeout (in milliseconds)
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	 -s                          suppresses the FET firmware update prompt         
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	                                                                               
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	If not all options are initialized the demo will use default options and return
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	a warning!                                                                     
Fri Dec 06 17:34:17 2013:	*******************************************************************************
